\DoxyCodeLine{560 \textcolor{keyword}{using }std::size\_t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{561 }
\DoxyCodeLine{562 DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \textcolor{keyword}{extern} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} is\_running\_in\_test;}
\DoxyCodeLine{563 }
\DoxyCodeLine{564 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{565 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE unsigned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{566 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{567 }
\DoxyCodeLine{568 \textcolor{comment}{// A 24 byte string class (can be as small as 17 for x64 and 13 for x86) that can hold strings with length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{569 \textcolor{comment}{// of up to 23 chars on the stack before going on the heap -\/ the last byte of the buffer is used for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{570 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ "{}is small"{} bit -\/ the highest bit -\/ if "{}0"{} then it is small -\/ otherwise its "{}1"{} (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{571 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ capacity left before going on the heap -\/ using the lowest 5 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{572 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ 2 bits are left unused -\/ the second and third highest ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{573 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ acts as a null terminator if strlen() is 23 (24 including the null terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{574 \textcolor{comment}{//              and the "{}is small"{} bit remains "{}0"{} ("{}as well as the capacity left"{}) so its OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{575 \textcolor{comment}{// Idea taken from this lecture about the string implementation of facebook/folly -\/ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{576 \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{577 \textcolor{comment}{// TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{578 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ optimizations -\/ like not deleting memory unnecessarily in operator= and etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{579 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ resize/reserve/clear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{580 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{581 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ back/front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{582 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ iterator stuff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{583 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ find \& friends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{584 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ push\_back/pop\_back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{585 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ assign/insert/erase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{586 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ relational operators as free functions -\/ taking const char* as one of the params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{587 \textcolor{keyword}{class }DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \mbox{\hyperlink{classdoctest_1_1String}{String}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{588 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{744         DT\_REQUIRE = is\_normal | is\_require,}
\DoxyCodeLine{745 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1375 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    DOCTEST\_NOINLINE SFINAE\_OP(Result,op) operator op(R\&\& rhs) \{                                   \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    bool res = op\_macro(doctest::detail::forward<const L>(lhs), doctest::detail::forward<R>(rhs)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1377 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(m\_at \& assertType::is\_false)                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            res = !res;                                                                            \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        if(!res || doctest::getContextOptions()-\/>success)                                          \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1380 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            return Result(res, stringifyBinaryExpr(lhs, op\_str, rhs));                             \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        return Result(res);                                                                        \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1893         \textcolor{comment}{// kept here just for backwards-\/compatibility -\/ the comma operator should be preferred now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895         \mbox{\hyperlink{structdoctest_1_1detail_1_1MessageBuilder}{MessageBuilder}}\& operator<<(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& in) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} this-\/>operator,(in); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1897         \textcolor{comment}{// the `,` operator has the lowest operator precedence -\/ if `<<` is used by the user then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898         \textcolor{comment}{// the `,` operator will be called last which is not what we want and thus the `*` operator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899         \textcolor{comment}{// is used first (has higher operator precedence compared to `<<`) so that we guarantee that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900         \textcolor{comment}{// an operator of the MessageBuilder class is called first before the rest of the parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902         \mbox{\hyperlink{structdoctest_1_1detail_1_1MessageBuilder}{MessageBuilder}}\& operator*(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& in) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} this-\/>operator,(in); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1904         \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} log();}

\DoxyCodeLine{3416 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3418     \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = T;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421     \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = std::atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3424 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS) || defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426     \textcolor{keyword}{using }MultiLaneAtomic = Atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428     \textcolor{comment}{// Provides a multilane implementation of an atomic variable that supports add, sub, load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429     \textcolor{comment}{// store. Instead of using a single atomic variable, this splits up into multiple ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430     \textcolor{comment}{// each sitting on a separate cache line. The goal is to provide a speedup when most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431     \textcolor{comment}{// operations are modifying. It achieves this with two properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433     \textcolor{comment}{// * Multiple atomics are used, so chance of congestion from the same atomic is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434     \textcolor{comment}{// * Each atomic sits on a separate cache line, so false sharing is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436     \textcolor{comment}{// The disadvantage is that there is a small overhead due to the use of TLS, and load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437     \textcolor{comment}{// is slower because all atomics have to be accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439     \textcolor{keyword}{class }MultiLaneAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441         \textcolor{keyword}{struct }CacheLineAlignedAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443             Atomic<T> atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(Atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446         CacheLineAlignedAtomic m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3448         \textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(CacheLineAlignedAtomic) == DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449                       \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}guarantee one atomic takes exactly one cache line"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3451     \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452         T operator++() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1) + 1; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3454         T operator++(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3456         T fetch\_add(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_add(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3460         T fetch\_sub(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_sub(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3464         \textcolor{keyword}{operator} T() const DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} load(); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3466         T load(std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) \textcolor{keyword}{const} DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467             \textcolor{keyword}{auto} result = T();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto} \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469                 result += c.atomic.load(order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3474         T operator=(T desired) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{comment}{// lgtm [cpp/assignment-\/does-\/not-\/return-\/this]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475             store(desired);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} desired;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3479         \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} store(T desired, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480             \textcolor{comment}{// first value becomes desired"{}, all others become 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482                 c.atomic.store(desired, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483                 desired = \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3487     \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488         \textcolor{comment}{// Each thread has a different atomic that it operates on. If more than NumLanes threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489         \textcolor{comment}{// use this, some will use the same atomic. So performance will degrade a bit, but still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490         \textcolor{comment}{// everything will work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492         \textcolor{comment}{// The logic here is a bit tricky. The call should be as fast as possible, so that there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493         \textcolor{comment}{// is minimal to no overhead in determining the correct atomic for the current thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495         \textcolor{comment}{// 1. A global static counter laneCounter counts continuously up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496         \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Each successive thread will use modulo operation of that counter so it gets an atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497         \textcolor{comment}{//    assigned in a round-\/robin fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498         \textcolor{comment}{// 3. This tlsLaneIdx is stored in the thread local data, so it is directly available with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499         \textcolor{comment}{//    little overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         Atomic<T>\& myAtomic() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501             \textcolor{keyword}{static} Atomic<size\_t> laneCounter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502             DOCTEST\_THREAD\_LOCAL \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} tlsLaneIdx =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503                     laneCounter++ \% DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3505             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} m\_atomics[tlsLaneIdx].atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507     \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3510     \textcolor{comment}{// this holds both parameters from the command line and runtime data for tests}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511     \textcolor{keyword}{struct }ContextState : ContextOptions, TestRunStats, CurrentTestCaseStats}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513         MultiLaneAtomic<int> numAssertsCurrentTest\_atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514         MultiLaneAtomic<int> numAssertsFailedCurrentTest\_atomic;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3546             seconds = timer.getElapsedSeconds();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3548             \textcolor{comment}{// update the non-\/atomic counters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549             numAsserts += numAssertsCurrentTest\_atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550             numAssertsFailed += numAssertsFailedCurrentTest\_atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551             numAssertsCurrentTest       = numAssertsCurrentTest\_atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3552             numAssertsFailedCurrentTest = numAssertsFailedCurrentTest\_atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3553 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3554             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(numAssertsFailedCurrentTest)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555                 failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::AssertFailure;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3557             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(Approx(currentTest-\/>m\_timeout).epsilon(DBL\_EPSILON) != 0 \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558                Approx(seconds).epsilon(DBL\_EPSILON) > currentTest-\/>m\_timeout)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559                 failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::Timeout;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3560 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3561             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(currentTest-\/>m\_should\_fail) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3562                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(failure\_flags) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3563                     failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::ShouldHaveFailedAndDid;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3564                 \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3565                     failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::ShouldHaveFailedButDidnt;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3567             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(failure\_flags \&\& currentTest-\/>m\_may\_fail) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3569             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(currentTest-\/>m\_expected\_failures > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(numAssertsFailedCurrentTest == currentTest-\/>m\_expected\_failures) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571                     failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::FailedExactlyNumTimes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572                 \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3573                     failure\_flags |= TestCaseFailureReason::DidntFailExactlyNumTimes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3577             \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} ok\_to\_fail = (TestCaseFailureReason::ShouldHaveFailedAndDid \& failure\_flags) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{3578                               (TestCaseFailureReason::CouldHaveFailedAndDid \& failure\_flags) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579                               (TestCaseFailureReason::FailedExactlyNumTimes \& failure\_flags);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3581             \textcolor{comment}{// if any subcase has failed -\/ the whole test case has failed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3582             testCaseSuccess = !(failure\_flags \&\& !ok\_to\_fail);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3662 String\& String::operator+=(\textcolor{keyword}{const} String\& other) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663     \textcolor{keyword}{const} size\_type my\_old\_size = size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664     \textcolor{keyword}{const} size\_type other\_size  = other.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665     \textcolor{keyword}{const} size\_type total\_size  = my\_old\_size + other\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isOnStack()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(total\_size < len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668             \textcolor{comment}{// append to the current stack space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669             memcpy(buf + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670             \textcolor{comment}{// NOLINTNEXTLINE(clang-\/analyzer-\/cplusplus.NewDeleteLeaks)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671             setLast(last -\/ total\_size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673             \textcolor{comment}{// alloc new chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* temp = \textcolor{keyword}{new} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}[total\_size + 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675             \textcolor{comment}{// copy current data to new location before writing in the union}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676             memcpy(temp, buf, my\_old\_size); \textcolor{comment}{// skip the +1 ('\(\backslash\)0') for speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677             \textcolor{comment}{// update data in union}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678             setOnHeap();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679             data.size     = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680             data.capacity = data.size + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681             data.ptr      = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682             \textcolor{comment}{// transfer the rest of the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(data.capacity > total\_size) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687             \textcolor{comment}{// append to the current heap block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688             data.size = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691             \textcolor{comment}{// resize}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692             data.capacity *= 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(data.capacity <= total\_size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694                 data.capacity = total\_size + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695             \textcolor{comment}{// alloc new chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* temp = \textcolor{keyword}{new} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}[data.capacity];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697             \textcolor{comment}{// copy current data to new location before releasing it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698             memcpy(temp, data.ptr, my\_old\_size); \textcolor{comment}{// skip the +1 ('\(\backslash\)0') for speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699             \textcolor{comment}{// release old chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700             \textcolor{keyword}{delete}[] data.ptr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701             \textcolor{comment}{// update the rest of the union members}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702             data.size = total\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703             data.ptr  = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704             \textcolor{comment}{// transfer the rest of the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705             memcpy(data.ptr + my\_old\_size, other.c\_str(), other\_size + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4110     \textcolor{keyword}{using namespace }detail;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4111     \textcolor{comment}{// matching of a string against a wildcard mask (case sensitivity configurable) taken from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4112     \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1088/Wildcard-\/string-\/compare-\/globbing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4113     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} wildcmp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* wild, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4114         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* cp = str;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4115         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4116 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4117         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}((*str) \&\& (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4118             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild != *str) : (tolower(*wild) != tolower(*str))) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{4119                (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4120                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4121             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4122             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4123             str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4124         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4125 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4126         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4127             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4128                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(!*++wild) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4129                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4130                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4131                 mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4132                 cp = str + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4133             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild == *str) : (tolower(*wild) == tolower(*str))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4134                       (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4135                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4136                 str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4137             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4138                 wild = mp;   }
\DoxyCodeLine{4139                 str  = cp++; }
\DoxyCodeLine{4140             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4141         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4142 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4143         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4144             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4145         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4146         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} !*wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4147     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4148 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4541     \textcolor{comment}{// Returns true if the current process is being debugged (either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4542     \textcolor{comment}{// running under the debugger or has a debugger attached post facto).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4543     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isDebuggerActive() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4544         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}        mib[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4545         kinfo\_proc info;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4546         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}     size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4547         \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the flags so that, if sysctl fails for some bizarre}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4548         \textcolor{comment}{// reason, we get a predictable result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4549         info.kp\_proc.p\_flag = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4550         \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize mib, which tells sysctl the info we want, in this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4551         \textcolor{comment}{// we're looking for information about a specific process ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4552         mib[0] = CTL\_KERN;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4553         mib[1] = KERN\_PROC;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4554         mib[2] = KERN\_PROC\_PID;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4555         mib[3] = getpid();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4556         \textcolor{comment}{// Call sysctl.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4557         size = \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(info);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4558         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(sysctl(mib, DOCTEST\_COUNTOF(mib), \&info, \&size, 0, 0) != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4559             std::cerr << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)nCall to sysctl failed -\/ unable to determine if debugger is active **\(\backslash\)n"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4560             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4561         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4562         \textcolor{comment}{// We're being debugged if the P\_TRACED flag is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4563         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ((info.kp\_proc.p\_flag \& P\_TRACED) != 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4565 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif DOCTEST\_MSVC || defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) || defined(\_\_MINGW64\_\_)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4680         FatalConditionHandler() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4681             isSet = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4682             \textcolor{comment}{// 32k seems enough for doctest to handle stack overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4683             \textcolor{comment}{// but the value was found experimentally, so there is no strong guarantee}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4684             guaranteeSize = 32 * 1024;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4685             \textcolor{comment}{// Register an unhandled exception filter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4686             previousTop = SetUnhandledExceptionFilter(handleException);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4687             \textcolor{comment}{// Pass in guarantee size to be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4688             SetThreadStackGuarantee(\&guaranteeSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4689 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4690             \textcolor{comment}{// On Windows uncaught exceptions from another thread, exceptions from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4691             \textcolor{comment}{// destructors, or calls to std::terminate are not a SEH exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4692 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4693             \textcolor{comment}{// The terminal handler gets called when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4694             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4695             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4696             original\_terminate\_handler = std::get\_terminate();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4697             std::set\_terminate([]() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4698                 reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Terminate handler called"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4699                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4700                     DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4701                 std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE); \textcolor{comment}{// explicitly exit -\/ otherwise the SIGABRT handler may be called as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4702             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4704             \textcolor{comment}{// SIGABRT is raised when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4705             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4706             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4707             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an uncaught exception is thrown FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708             prev\_sigabrt\_handler = std::signal(SIGABRT, [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} signal) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4709                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(signal == SIGABRT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4710                     reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SIGABRT -\/ Abort (abnormal termination) signal"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4712                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4713                     std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4714                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4715             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4717             \textcolor{comment}{// The following settings are taken from google test, and more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4718             \textcolor{comment}{// specifically from UnitTest::Run() inside of gtest.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4719 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4720             \textcolor{comment}{// the user does not want to see pop-\/up dialogs about crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721             prev\_error\_mode\_1 = SetErrorMode(SEM\_FAILCRITICALERRORS | SEM\_NOALIGNMENTFAULTEXCEPT |}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722                                              SEM\_NOGPFAULTERRORBOX | SEM\_NOOPENFILEERRORBOX);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723             \textcolor{comment}{// This forces the abort message to go to stderr in all circumstances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4724             prev\_error\_mode\_2 = \_set\_error\_mode(\_OUT\_TO\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4725             \textcolor{comment}{// In the debug version, Visual Studio pops up a separate dialog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4726             \textcolor{comment}{// offering a choice to debug the aborted program -\/ we want to disable that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727             prev\_abort\_behavior = \_set\_abort\_behavior(0x0, \_WRITE\_ABORT\_MSG | \_CALL\_REPORTFAULT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728             \textcolor{comment}{// In debug mode, the Windows CRT can crash with an assertion over invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729             \textcolor{comment}{// input (e.g. passing an invalid file descriptor). The default handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730             \textcolor{comment}{// for these assertions is to pop up a dialog and wait for user input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731             \textcolor{comment}{// Instead ask the CRT to dump such assertions to stderr non-\/interactively.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5177     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} XmlEncode::encodeTo( \mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os )\textcolor{keyword}{ const }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5178         \textcolor{comment}{// Apostrophe escaping not necessary if we always use "{} to write attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5179         \textcolor{comment}{// (see: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5180 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5181         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}( std::size\_t idx = 0; idx < m\_str.size(); ++ idx ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5182             uchar c = m\_str[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5183             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5184             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'<'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&lt;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5185             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\&'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&amp;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5186 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5187             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'>'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5188                 \textcolor{comment}{// See: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5189                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx > 2 \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'} \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{5190                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&gt;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5191                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5192                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5193                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5194 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5195             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5196                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_forWhat == ForAttributes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5197                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&quot;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5198                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5199                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5200                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5201 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5202             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5203                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check for control characters and invalid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5205                 \textcolor{comment}{// Escape control characters in standard ascii}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5206                 \textcolor{comment}{// see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/404107/why-\/are-\/control-\/characters-\/illegal-\/in-\/xml-\/1-\/0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5207                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x09 || (c > 0x0D \&\& c < 0x20) || c == 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5208                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5209                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5210                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5211 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5212                 \textcolor{comment}{// Plain ASCII: Write it to stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5213                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5214                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5215                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5216                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5217 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5218                 \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/8 territory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5219                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check if the encoding is valid and if it is not, hex escape bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5220                 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: We do not check the exact decoded values for validity, only the encoding format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5221                 \textcolor{comment}{// First check that this bytes is a valid lead byte:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5222                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means that it is not encoded as 1111 1XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5223                 \textcolor{comment}{// Or as 10XX XXXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5224                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c <  0xC0 ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5225                     c >= 0xF8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5226                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5227                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5228                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5229 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5230                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} encBytes = trailingBytes(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5231                 \textcolor{comment}{// Are there enough bytes left to avoid accessing out-\/of-\/bounds memory?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5232                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx + encBytes -\/ 1 >= m\_str.size()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5233                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5234                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5235                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5236                 \textcolor{comment}{// The header is valid, check data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5237                 \textcolor{comment}{// The next encBytes bytes must together be a valid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5238                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means: bitpattern 10XX XXXX and the extracted value is sane (ish)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5239                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} valid = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5240                 uint32\_t value = headerValue(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5241                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 1; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5242                     uchar nc = m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5243                     valid \&= ((nc \& 0xC0) == 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5244                     value = (value << 6) | (nc \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5245                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5246 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5247                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (}
\DoxyCodeLine{5248                     \textcolor{comment}{// Wrong bit pattern of following bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5249                     (!valid) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5250                     \textcolor{comment}{// Overlong encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5251                     (value < 0x80) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5252                     (                 value < 0x800   \&\& encBytes > 2) || \textcolor{comment}{// removed "{}0x80 <= value \&\&"{} because redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5253                     (0x800 < value \&\& value < 0x10000 \&\& encBytes > 3) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5254                     \textcolor{comment}{// Encoded value out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5255                     (value >= 0x110000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5256                     ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5257                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5258                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5259                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5260 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5261                 \textcolor{comment}{// If we got here, this is in fact a valid(ish) utf-\/8 sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5262                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 0; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5263                     os << m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5264                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5265                 idx += encBytes -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5266                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5267             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5268         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5269     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5270 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5271     \mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& operator << ( \mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os, XmlEncode \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& xmlEncode ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5272         xmlEncode.encodeTo( os );}
\DoxyCodeLine{5273         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} os;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5274     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6449     \textcolor{comment}{// the implementation of parseOption()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6450     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} parseOptionImpl(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} argc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* \textcolor{keyword}{const}* argv, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* pattern, String* value) \{}
